\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{00001\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ SHAPES\ ::\ https://github.com/prideout/par}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00002\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Simple\ C\ library\ for\ creation\ and\ manipulation\ of\ triangle\ meshes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00003\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00004\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ API\ is\ divided\ into\ three\ sections:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00005\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00006\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ -\/\ Generators.\ \ Create\ parametric\ surfaces,\ platonic\ solids,\ etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00007\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ -\/\ Queries.\ \ \ \ \ Ask\ a\ mesh\ for\ its\ axis-\/aligned\ bounding\ box,\ etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00008\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ -\/\ Transforms.\ \ Rotate\ a\ mesh,\ merge\ it\ with\ another,\ add\ normals,\ etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00009\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00010\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ In\ addition\ to\ the\ comment\ block\ above\ each\ function\ declaration,\ the\ API}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00011\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ has\ informal\ documentation\ here:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00012\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00013\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ https://prideout.net/shapes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00014\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00015\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ For\ our\ purposes,\ a\ "{}mesh"{}\ is\ a\ list\ of\ points\ and\ a\ list\ of\ triangles;\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00016\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ former\ is\ a\ flattened\ list\ of\ three-\/tuples\ (32-\/bit\ floats)\ and\ the\ latter\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00017\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ also\ a\ flattened\ list\ of\ three-\/tuples\ (16-\/bit\ uints).\ \ Triangles\ are\ always}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00018\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ oriented\ such\ that\ their\ front\ face\ winds\ counter-\/clockwise.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00019\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00020\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Optionally,\ meshes\ can\ contain\ 3D\ normals\ (one\ per\ vertex),\ and\ 2D\ texture}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00021\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ coordinates\ (one\ per\ vertex).\ \ That's\ it!\ \ If\ you\ need\ something\ fancier,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00022\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ look\ elsewhere.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00023\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00024\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ MIT\ License}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00025\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Copyright\ (c)\ 2015\ Philip\ Rideout}}
